  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_d03e8b42-f188-468b-8f1c-52ba34256234'

<span id="freeTextContainer9535252953702238471">Awakening Inner Guru is a clear and straightforward guide to awaken the light within. The book is about awakening your inner wisdom, inner power, inner beauty, your inner self. Living a fulfilling life is a skill that requires both practice and understanding. This book provides both.   <span id="freeText9535252953702238471" style="display:none">Awakening Inner Guru is a clear and straightforward guide to awaken the light within. The book is about awakening your inner wisdom, inner power, inner beauty, your inner self. Living a fulfilling life is a skill that requires both practice and understanding. This book provides both. It is a gem! It can be used for inspiration, or instruction. It can be read countless times for added insight. You may also enjoy reading this book if you really want to explore the full potential of your inner strength. It offers a very down-to-earth approach to understanding, in detail and simple language. For those who are truly interested to attain spiritual freedom and fulfillment in every sphere of life, this book is a practical and personal manual.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer7527089477004996426">This is a warm, inspiring and, above all, practical book. Its gentle wisdom will guide you through the ups and downs of contemporary living, such as emotional healing, problems with relationships and the difficulties of achieving balance in life. <br/><br/>The book is about awakening your inner wisdom, inner power, inner beauty, your inner self. <br/><br/>You may also enjoy reading this book if you really want to explore the full potential of your inner strength. <br/><br/>I found this book most inspiring. The writing style </span>
  <span id="freeText7527089477004996426" style="display:none">This is a warm, inspiring and, above all, practical book. Its gentle wisdom will guide you through the ups and downs of contemporary living, such as emotional healing, problems with relationships and the difficulties of achieving balance in life. <br /><br />The book is about awakening your inner wisdom, inner power, inner beauty, your inner self. <br /><br />You may also enjoy reading this book if you really want to explore the full potential of your inner strength. <br /><br />I found this book most inspiring. The writing style is inherently calming to me. This book is absolutely Great!!! Is very easy to read. The authors make the concept of Inner Awakening easy to understand. </span>

<div id="review_2526513231" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2526513231" />
    <a title="Tracey White" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/86615686-tracey-white"><img alt="Tracey White" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1536770040p2/86615686.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2526513231?book_show_action=true">Sep 11, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tracey White" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tracey White" href="/user/show/86615686-tracey-white">Tracey White</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2526513231" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11218314642572564363">This book is so enlightening. Sometimes we can get all caught up in the gloom and doom that goes on around us and forget to look up. <br/>This book came as a God-send. I am an undergrad student of philosophy and linguistics, a branch of the humanities. I was going through a personal problem for the last two years. This book has personally helped me triumph over many, many challenges. This is why I decided to write a review here.<br/>The study of modern science and philosophy can make people skeptic, becau</span>
  <span id="freeText11218314642572564363" style="display:none">This book is so enlightening. Sometimes we can get all caught up in the gloom and doom that goes on around us and forget to look up. <br />This book came as a God-send. I am an undergrad student of philosophy and linguistics, a branch of the humanities. I was going through a personal problem for the last two years. This book has personally helped me triumph over many, many challenges. This is why I decided to write a review here.<br />The study of modern science and philosophy can make people skeptic, because, often language is used in various cultures to create belief systems. A belief system is basically a set of instructions inculcated inside your brain based on language. These instructions help you navigate the stressful world around you so you can survive. We are psychologically wired to think our belief systems are accurate and experience deep stress if we find them to be inaccurate.<br /><br />Now, the trouble is, our belief systems are almost ALWAYS inaccurate. <br />When you study philosophy, you study belief systems about how the world works, and explore important questions like: 'Why I am here on Earth?', "is there a God?" or "What is consciousness?" You may not be surprised to find out that philosophy majors have not come up with answers to these questions, because there is always a case of counter argument. Much of the study of philosophy is the collection of vocabulary words to describe beliefs. In fact all our beliefs are based on language and language can never "touch reality", because language is just an arbitrary description of reality. It's like you can't accurately give describe exactly how the milk tastes to a person who had never drunk milk. <br />Scientists and academics in the millions have tried and tried and tried to find "the true belief" for thousands, maybe tens of thousands of years and we have not yet arrived at any truth. For the first time in my life I stumbled over a book of spirituality that doesn't require you to subscribe to a belief system. The best thing I like about the book is it doesn't preach any belief system. It just invites you to take the journey with an open mind.<br /><br />HOW THIS BOOK HAS PERSONALLY HELPED ME ? IT HELPED ME TO UNDERSTAND:<br /><br />1. I am A unique human being. God loves me and I have the right to love myself. <br /><br />2. No one can force me to do anything unless I choose to .<br /><br />3. I have all the power on earth within me. <br /><br />4. It’s possible to be authentic with yourself and others.<br /><br />5. Forgiveness is divine. When we forgive others we are not doing any favor to them. Rather, we are giving permissions to us to move forward and write a new chapter of our lives that is filled with goodness.<br /><br />Thanks, Banani. This book was all I needed to move forward in my life with an unbiased mind. </span>
  <a data-text-id="11218314642572564363" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer9299206943728495996">The main strengths of this books is that it doesn't promote only one kind of meditation. <br/>Banani Ray has explained all the different forms of meditation - from concentration meditation to contemplative, from focusing on breath to chakra meditation, from chants to self inquiry.   <span id="freeText9299206943728495996" style="display:none">The main strengths of this books is that it doesn't promote only one kind of meditation. <br />Banani Ray has explained all the different forms of meditation - from concentration meditation to contemplative, from focusing on breath to chakra meditation, from chants to self inquiry. This is extremely useful since different methods will appeal to different people and in the end meditation should not be about dogma - about following one method only, but about letting the mind settle down, irrespective of the method involved. Like an expert spiritual teacher she takes us through the journey. I highly recommend this book to anyone sincere to learn and practice.<br /><br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer192644652930770101">Insightful and practical guidebook on aligning your consciousness, your being to the energy of the Universe, so that you can effortlessly release your wish to the Universe, and learn to light the lamp within you, and let the Universe make things happen when the time is perfect. <br/><br/>The practice of forgiveness for the day, and the practice of silence are particularly useful to me. Thank you, Banani!<br/></span>

          </span>

<div id="review_3252359186" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3252359186" />
    <a title="Paweł Sikora" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/86000566-pawe-sikora"><img alt="Paweł Sikora" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/u_50x66-632230dc9882b4352d753eedf9396530.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3252359186?book_show_action=true">May 03, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Paweł Sikora" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Paweł Sikora" href="/user/show/86000566-pawe-sikora">Paweł Sikora</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer3252359186&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3252359186" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer239999712854481304">This book describes spiritual concepts which theoretically should not be describable in words and also gives very concrete guides and practices for finding something more inside you than your body and mind.<br/><br/>Authors say that you are not your mind or body but you are some kind of the unborn energy which is pure consciousness, inner guru, eternal bliss, soundless sound etc.<br/>When you learn to find that in yourself then you will feel infinite joy.<br/><br/>The good side of this book are tips to control your mind</span>
  <span id="freeText239999712854481304" style="display:none">This book describes spiritual concepts which theoretically should not be describable in words and also gives very concrete guides and practices for finding something more inside you than your body and mind.<br /><br />Authors say that you are not your mind or body but you are some kind of the unborn energy which is pure consciousness, inner guru, eternal bliss, soundless sound etc.<br />When you learn to find that in yourself then you will feel infinite joy.<br /><br />The good side of this book are tips to control your mind and live guidelines. Thanks to that you can learn to be calm and peaceful and not overreacting to difficult live situations. This is the ground for the more advanced practices for finding the inner bliss.<br /><br />The authors promise very great benefits of Awakening this inner guru. Nevertheless they don't give any evidence or examples that anyone did that. This makes me sceptical and unmotivated to take the advanced practices seriously.</span>
  <a data-text-id="239999712854481304" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('c3IUd7NS8MFcjpJklQxnH/n/lVJ9dtFjCHr8iRss/7oXWkCaL78YL1f/cm+TYFDEllvHHACBwTrrz7p5iqKHyg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('mB9tXyvFaA93gdcgXbe/13YiGhBWS+NX5PqaLmTBueP8NzmytyiA4XzwNytb24gMGYZIXiu88w4HT9ze9U/Bkw==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

Om is the mantra of integration; integration of individual with<\/span>\n  <span id=\"freeText13829613989265493176\" style=\"display:none\">The book provides some powerful Om chanting and meditation techniques to bring balance health and harmony in life. In Eastern religions, Om (AUM) is considered as the most sacred mantra. Om is the mantra of integration; integration of individual with the Whole. Om is the mantra of harmony and celebration. Om is the mantra to access the Supreme Divinity residing within us. In this book Amit Ray describes several Om chanting and Om meditation methods in detail in a lucid and plain English. Om chanting and meditations have healing effects on the body and the mind. This book is a step-by-step guide to practise meditations with the Om. As you practise, a long-lasting sense of well-being manifests in your life. You will notice a sense of joyfulness entering your life along with an ability to appreciate the many gifts that surround you. <div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer13014829427462021813">Banani Ray is a mystic, spiritual guide and an authority on meditation and transformation of consciousness. She teaches Om Inner Sun Meditation, a powerful but simple meditation technique that brings out your inner potential, activates the solar energy in your body, balances the Chakras and enlighten the mind. She is author of several books on meditation, mysticism and infinite human potential. He</span>
  <span id="freeText13014829427462021813" style="display:none">Banani Ray is a mystic, spiritual guide and an authority on meditation and transformation of consciousness. She teaches Om Inner Sun Meditation, a powerful but simple meditation technique that brings out your inner potential, activates the solar energy in your body, balances the Chakras and enlighten the mind. She is author of several books on meditation, mysticism and infinite human potential. Her passion is to de-mystify meditation and teach meditation as a simple practice for improving lives. She is an outstanding meditation master and spiritual guide who teaches how with a simple daily meditation technique we can reprogram our consciousness and biology to improve health, wealth, relationship and every aspect of our lives. Simple, yet profound and effective, her teaching integrates her knowledge of modern neuroscience, biology, psychology and epigenetics with ancient wisdom revealed to her through deep meditation.<br /><br />While she was teaching in a women's college, she experienced an awakening, and underwent a massive inner transformation, which led her to undertake deep spiritual practices in the quest for realization of the ultimate truth. For the next nine years, she devoted all her time to meditation.<br />Ultimately, her quest motivated her to undertake austere spiritual practices and self-enquiry in solitude. For several years, she lived in Himalaya with her husband Amit Ray, living a life dedicated to meditation and spiritual practices. Over the years, a series of mystic experiences opened up for her the door for profound realization of the underlying connectedness and oneness of all beings. She started living her realization, sharing her wisdom through her writings and teaching.</span>
